These include reskinning all the apps controls and scores to any magic colour, adding drop shadows to scores, image processing to darken the wallpaper to increase contrast and most unique of all - new resizable glass overlays for controls and scores with customisable blur ( based on DirectX gaming technology).\r\n\r\nFor timed matches use a highly accurate timer with verbal timer announcements/warnings plus Time on the Round \"Gong\" alarm. Fully settable, continues working when receiving phone calls, lockscreening or switching between apps.\r\n\r\nTimed matches can also use the \"Go To Turns\" Timeout Management, triggered when timer runs out or available directly at any time. No need to remember which extra turn we are on, how many are left overall or how many turns you have to try and win. An animated and verbal feature walks you through it all. \r\n\r\nNew \"Recorded Games Stats\" feature optionally records all game wins.
